Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ) What material is the butterfly wing romper made of? This romper is crafted from a soft cotton and spandex blend, featuring a breathable textured weave ideal for summer weather. Is the back bow removable? The oversized chiffon butterfly bow is securely attached to ensure the silhouette stays in place during movement and play. Why is the size tag on the outside? To protect your baby's delicate skin from irritation and scratching, we purposely sew the size tags on the exterior of the garment. How should I wash this outfit? We recommend a gentle cold wash in a mesh laundry bag and hanging to dry to preserve the 3D flowers and chiffon bow.
